| <span data-ttu-id="4f5cd-446">進入</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f5cd-446">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4f5cd-447">值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f5cd-447">Value</span></span> |
